# Awesome GitHub Copilot
# GitHub Copilot 精选资源

> A community-driven collection of custom agents, instructions, and skills to enhance GitHub Copilot experiences across various domains, languages, and use cases.
> 一个社区驱动的集合，包含自定义代理、指令和技能，旨在增强 GitHub Copilot 在各种领域、语言和使用场景下的体验。

## Overview
## 概述

This repository provides resources to customize and enhance GitHub Copilot:
本仓库提供了用于自定义和增强 GitHub Copilot 的资源：

- **Agents**: Specialized GitHub Copilot agents that integrate with MCP servers
- **代理**：与 MCP 服务器集成的专业化 GitHub Copilot 代理
- **Instructions**: Coding standards and best practices applied to specific file patterns
- **指令**：应用于特定文件模式的编码标准和最佳实践
- **Skills**: Self-contained folders with instructions and bundled resources for specialized tasks
- **技能**：包含指令和打包资源的独立文件夹，用于执行专业化任务
- **Learning Hub**: Curated guides, tutorials, and reference material published on the website
- **学习中心**：在网站上发布的精选指南、教程和参考资料

## Learning Hub
## 学习中心

- [Agentic Workflows](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/agentic-workflows/): Learn what GitHub Agentic Workflows are, how to use community workflows from Awesome Copilot, and how to contribute your own.
- [代理式工作流](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/agentic-workflows/)：了解什么是 GitHub 代理式工作流，如何使用 Awesome Copilot 的社区工作流，以及如何贡献你自己的工作流。
- [Agents and Subagents](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/agents-and-subagents/): Learn how delegated subagents differ from primary agents, when to use them, and how to launch them in VS Code and Copilot CLI.
- [代理与子代理](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/agents-and-subagents/)：了解委托子代理与主代理的区别，何时使用它们，以及如何在 VS Code 和 Copilot CLI 中启动它们。
- [Automating with Hooks](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/automating-with-hooks/): Learn how to use hooks to automate lifecycle events like formatting, linting, and governance checks during Copilot agent sessions.
- [使用钩子实现自动化](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/automating-with-hooks/)：了解如何使用钩子在 Copilot 代理会话期间自动化生命周期事件，如格式化、代码检查和治理检查。
- [Before/After Customization Examples](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/before-after-customization-examples/): See real-world transformations showing how custom agents, skills, and instructions dramatically improve GitHub Copilot effectiveness.
- [自定义前后对比示例](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/before-after-customization-examples/)：查看真实案例，展示自定义代理、技能和指令如何显著提升 GitHub Copilot 的效果。
- [Building Custom Agents](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/building-custom-agents/): Learn how to create specialized GitHub Copilot agents with custom personas, tool integrations, and domain expertise.
- [构建自定义代理](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/building-custom-agents/)：了解如何创建具有自定义角色、工具集成和领域专业知识的专用 GitHub Copilot 代理。
- [GitHub Copilot CLI for Beginners](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/): A source-faithful mirror of the companion GitHub Copilot CLI for Beginners course.
- [GitHub Copilot CLI 初学者指南](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/)：配套 GitHub Copilot CLI 初学者课程的忠实源镜像。

- [01 · First Steps](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/01-setup-and-first-steps/): Experience your first GitHub Copilot CLI demos and learn the three main interaction modes.
- [01 · 初步操作](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/01-setup-and-first-steps/)：体验你的第一个 GitHub Copilot CLI 演示，并了解三种主要交互模式。
- [02 · Context and Conversations](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/02-context-and-conversations/): Learn how to give Copilot CLI richer context and build stronger multi-turn conversations.

- [03 · Development Workflows](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/03-development-workflows/): Mirror the source development workflow chapter covering review, debugging, testing, and git support.

- [04 · Create Specialized AI Assistants](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/04-agents-and-custom-instructions/): Mirror the source chapter on custom agents and custom instructions for GitHub Copilot CLI.

- [05 · Automate Repetitive Tasks](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/cli-for-beginners/05-skills/): Mirror the source chapter on skills that load automatically for repeated GitHub Copilot CLI workflows.

- [Copilot Configuration Basics](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/copilot-configuration-basics/): Learn how to configure GitHub Copilot at user, workspace, and repository levels to optimize your AI-assisted development experience.

- [Creating Effective Skills](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/creating-effective-skills/): Master the art of writing reusable, shareable skill folders that deliver consistent results across your team.

- [Defining Custom Instructions](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/defining-custom-instructions/): Learn how to create persistent, context-aware instructions that guide GitHub Copilot automatically across your codebase.
- [定义自定义指令](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/defining-custom-instructions/)：了解如何创建持久的、上下文感知的指令，在整个代码库中自动引导 GitHub Copilot。
- [GitHub Copilot Terminology Glossary](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/github-copilot-terminology-glossary/): A quick reference guide defining common GitHub Copilot and platform-specific terms.
- [GitHub Copilot 术语表](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/github-copilot-terminology-glossary/)：定义常见 GitHub Copilot 和平台特定术语的快速参考指南。
- [Installing and Using Plugins](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/installing-and-using-plugins/): Learn how to find, install, and manage plugins that extend GitHub Copilot CLI with reusable agents, skills, hooks, and integrations.
- [安装和使用插件](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/installing-and-using-plugins/)：了解如何查找、安装和管理扩展 GitHub Copilot CLI 的插件，包括可复用的代理、技能、钩子和集成。
- [Understanding Copilot Context](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/understanding-copilot-context/): Learn how GitHub Copilot uses context from your code, workspace, and conversation to generate relevant suggestions.
- [理解 Copilot 上下文](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/understanding-copilot-context/)：了解 GitHub Copilot 如何利用代码、工作区和对话中的上下文来生成相关建议。
- [Understanding MCP Servers](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/understanding-mcp-servers/): Learn how Model Context Protocol servers extend GitHub Copilot with access to external tools, databases, and APIs.
- [理解 MCP 服务器](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/understanding-mcp-servers/)：了解模型上下文协议服务器如何通过访问外部工具、数据库和 API 来扩展 GitHub Copilot 的能力。
- [Using the Copilot Coding Agent](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/using-copilot-coding-agent/): Learn how to use GitHub Copilot coding agent to autonomously work on issues, generate pull requests, and automate development tasks.
- [使用 Copilot 编码代理](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/using-copilot-coding-agent/)：了解如何使用 GitHub Copilot 编码代理来自主处理 issue、生成 pull request 和自动化开发任务。
- [What are Agents, Skills, and Instructions](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/what-are-agents-skills-instructions/): Understand the primary customization primitives that extend GitHub Copilot for specific workflows.
- [代理、技能和指令是什么](https://awesome-copilot.github.com/learning-hub/what-are-agents-skills-instructions/)：理解扩展 GitHub Copilot 以适应特定工作流的主要自定义原语。

## Agents
## 代理

- [.NET Self Learning Architect](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/dotnet-self-learning-architect.agent.md): Senior .NET architect for complex delivery: designs .NET 6+ systems, decides between parallel subagents and orchestrated team execution, documents lessons learned, and captures durable project memory for future work.
- [.NET 自学习架构师](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/dotnet-self-learning-architect.agent.md)：面向复杂交付的高级 .NET 架构师：设计 .NET 6+ 系统，在并行子代理和编排团队执行之间做出决策，记录经验教训，并捕获持久的项目记忆以用于未来工作。
- [.NET Upgrade](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/dotnet-upgrade.agent.md): Perform janitorial tasks on C#/.NET code including cleanup, modernization, and tech debt remediation.
- [.NET 升级](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/dotnet-upgrade.agent.md)：对 C#/.NET 代码执行清理维护任务，包括代码清理、现代化和技术债务修复。
- [Accessibility Expert](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/accessibility.agent.md): Expert assistant for web accessibility (WCAG 2.1/2.2), inclusive UX, and a11y testing
- [无障碍专家](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/accessibility.agent.md)：Web 无障碍（WCAG 2.1/2.2）、包容性用户体验和无障碍测试的专家助手
- [Accessibility Runtime Tester](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/accessibility-runtime-tester.agent.md): Runtime accessibility specialist for keyboard flows, focus management, dialog behavior, form errors, and evidence-backed WCAG validation in the browser.
- [无障碍运行时测试器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/accessibility-runtime-tester.agent.md)：运行时无障碍专家，专注于键盘流程、焦点管理、对话框行为、表单错误以及浏览器中有据可查的 WCAG 验证。
- [ADR Generator](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/adr-generator.agent.md): Expert agent for creating comprehensive Architectural Decision Records (ADRs) with structured formatting optimized for AI consumption and human readability.
- [ADR 生成器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/adr-generator.agent.md)：用于创建全面架构决策记录 (ADR) 的专家代理，采用针对 AI 消费和人类可读性优化的结构化格式。
- [AEM Front End Specialist](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/aem-frontend-specialist.agent.md): Expert assistant for developing AEM components using HTL, Tailwind CSS, and Figma-to-code workflows with design system integration
- [AEM 前端专家](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/aem-frontend-specialist.agent.md)：使用 HTL、Tailwind CSS 和 Figma 转代码工作流开发 AEM 组件并集成设计系统的专家助手
- [Agent Governance Reviewer](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/agent-governance-reviewer.agent.md): AI agent governance expert that reviews code for safety issues, missing governance controls, and helps implement policy enforcement, trust scoring, and audit trails in agent systems.
- [代理治理审查员](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/agent-governance-reviewer.agent.md)：AI 代理治理专家，审查代码中的安全问题、缺失的治理控制，并帮助在代理系统中实施策略执行、信任评分和审计追踪。
- [Ai Readiness Reporter](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-readiness-reporter.agent.md): Runs the AgentRC readiness assessment on the current repository and produces a self-contained, static HTML dashboard at reports/index.html. Explains every readiness pillar, the maturity level, and an actionable remediation plan, framed by AgentRC measure → generate → maintain loop. Use when asked to assess, audit, score, report on, or visualise the AI readiness of a repo.
- [AI 就绪度报告器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-readiness-reporter.agent.md)：对当前仓库运行 AgentRC 就绪度评估，并在 reports/index.html 生成一个独立的静态 HTML 仪表板。解释每个就绪度支柱、成熟度级别和可操作的修复计划，以 AgentRC 测量 → 生成 → 维护的循环为框架。当被要求评估、审计、评分、报告或可视化仓库的 AI 就绪度时使用。
- [Ai Team Dev](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-team-dev.agent.md): AI development team agent (Nova, Sage, Milo). Use when: building features, writing application code, fixing bugs, implementing UI components, creating APIs, styling with CSS, writing database queries, or executing sprint plans. The team switches between frontend, backend, and design roles as needed.
- [AI 团队开发](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-team-dev.agent.md)：AI 开发团队代理（Nova、Sage、Milo）。适用于：构建功能、编写应用代码、修复 bug、实现 UI 组件、创建 API、CSS 样式设计、编写数据库查询或执行 Sprint 计划。团队根据需要在前端、后端和设计角色之间切换。
- [Ai Team Producer](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-team-producer.agent.md): AI team producer agent (Remy). Use when: planning sprints, creating PROJECT_BRIEF.md, triaging bugs, merging PRs, coordinating between dev and QA teams, filing GitHub Issues, writing sprint plans, running brainstorms, or recovering project context. NEVER writes application code.
- [AI 团队产品经理](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-team-producer.agent.md)：AI 团队产品经理代理（Remy）。适用于：规划 Sprint、创建 PROJECT_BRIEF.md、缺陷分流、合并 PR、协调开发和 QA 团队、提交 GitHub Issue、编写 Sprint 计划、组织头脑风暴或恢复项目上下文。绝不编写应用代码。
- [Ai Team Qa](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-team-qa.agent.md): AI QA engineer agent (Ivy). Use when: testing features, running E2E tests, playtesting, filing bug reports, writing test automation, creating QA sign-off documents, or verifying bug fixes. Reports bugs as GitHub Issues.
- [AI 团队 QA](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/ai-team-qa.agent.md)：AI QA 工程师代理（Ivy）。适用于：测试功能、运行端到端测试、体验测试、提交缺陷报告、编写测试自动化、创建 QA 签核文档或验证缺陷修复。以 GitHub Issue 形式报告缺陷。
- [Amplitude Experiment Implementation](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/amplitude-experiment-implementation.agent.md): This custom agent uses Amplitude's MCP tools to deploy new experiments inside of Amplitude, enabling seamless variant testing capabilities and rollout of product features.
- [Amplitude 实验实施](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/amplitude-experiment-implementation.agent.md)：此自定义代理使用 Amplitude 的 MCP 工具在 Amplitude 中部署新实验，实现无缝的变体测试能力和产品功能推出。
- [API Architect](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/api-architect.agent.md): Your role is that of an API architect. Help mentor the engineer by providing guidance, support, and working code.
- [API 架构师](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/api-architect.agent.md)：你的角色是 API 架构师。通过提供指导、支持和可运行的代码来帮助指导工程师。
- [Apify Integration Expert](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/apify-integration-expert.agent.md): Expert agent for integrating Apify Actors into codebases. Handles Actor selection, workflow design, implementation across JavaScript/TypeScript and Python, testing, and production-ready deployment.
- [Apify 集成专家](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/apify-integration-expert.agent.md)：将 Apify Actor 集成到代码库中的专家代理。处理 Actor 选择、工作流设计、跨 JavaScript/TypeScript 和 Python 的实现、测试以及生产就绪的部署。
- [Arch Linux Expert](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/arch-linux-expert.agent.md): Arch Linux specialist focused on pacman, rolling-release maintenance, and Arch-centric system administration workflows.
- [Arch Linux 专家](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/arch-linux-expert.agent.md)：Arch Linux 专家，专注于 pacman、滚动更新维护和以 Arch 为中心的系统管理工作流。
- [Arm Migration Agent](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/arm-migration.agent.md): Arm Cloud Migration Assistant accelerates moving x86 workloads to Arm infrastructure. It scans the repository for architecture assumptions, portability issues, container base image and dependency incompatibilities, and recommends Arm-optimized changes. It can drive multi-arch container builds, validate performance, and guide optimization, enabling smooth cross-platform deployment directly inside GitHub.
- [Arm 迁移代理](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/arm-migration.agent.md)：Arm 云迁移助手加速将 x86 工作负载迁移到 Arm 基础设施。它扫描仓库中的架构假设、可移植性问题、容器基础镜像和依赖不兼容性，并推荐针对 Arm 优化的变更。它可以驱动多架构容器构建、验证性能并指导优化，实现在 GitHub 内直接进行平滑的跨平台部署。
- [Atlassian Requirements to Jira](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/atlassian-requirements-to-jira.agent.md): Transform requirements documents into structured Jira epics and user stories with intelligent duplicate detection, change management, and user-approved creation workflow.
- [Atlassian 需求转 Jira](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/atlassian-requirements-to-jira.agent.md)：将需求文档转换为结构化的 Jira 史诗和用户故事，具有智能重复检测、变更管理和用户批准的创建工作流。
- [Aws Cloud Expert](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/aws-cloud-expert.agent.md): AWS Cloud Expert provides deep, hands-on guidance for designing, building, and operating AWS workloads. Covers the full AWS ecosystem — serverless, containers, databases, networking, IaC, security, and cost optimization — grounded in the AWS Well-Architected Framework.
- [AWS 云专家](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/aws-cloud-expert.agent.md)：AWS 云专家为设计、构建和运营 AWS 工作负载提供深入的实践指导。覆盖完整的 AWS 生态系统——无服务器、容器、数据库、网络、基础设施即代码、安全和成本优化——基于 AWS 良好架构框架。
- [Azure AVM Bicep mode](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/azure-verified-modules-bicep.agent.md): Create, update, or review Azure IaC in Bicep using Azure Verified Modules (AVM).
- [Azure AVM Bicep 模式](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/azure-verified-modules-bicep.agent.md)：使用 Azure 验证模块 (AVM) 以 Bicep 创建、更新或审查 Azure 基础设施即代码。
- [Azure AVM Terraform mode](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/azure-verified-modules-terraform.agent.md): Create, update, or review Azure IaC in Terraform using Azure Verified Modules (AVM).
- [Azure AVM Terraform 模式](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/azure-verified-modules-terraform.agent.md)：使用 Azure 验证模块 (AVM) 以 Terraform 创建、更新或审查 Azure 基础设施即代码。
- [Azure Iac Exporter](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/azure-iac-exporter.agent.md): Export existing Azure resources to Infrastructure as Code templates via Azure Resource Graph analysis, Azure Resource Manager API calls, and azure-iac-generator integration. Use this skill when the user asks to export, convert, migrate, or extract existing Azure resources to IaC templates (Bicep, ARM Templates, Terraform, Pulumi).
- [Azure IaC 导出器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/azure-iac-exporter.agent.md)：通过 Azure Resource Graph 分析、Azure Resource Manager API 调用和 azure-iac-generator 集成，将现有 Azure 资源导出为基础设施即代码模板。当用户要求将现有 Azure 资源导出、转换、迁移或提取为 IaC 模板（Bicep、ARM 模板、Terraform、Pulumi）时使用此技能。

- [React18 Batching Fixer](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/react18-batching-fixer.agent.md): Automatic batching regression specialist. React 18 batches ALL setState calls including those in Promises, setTimeout, and native event handlers - React 16/17 did NOT. Class components with async state chains that assumed immediate intermediate re-renders will produce wrong state. This agent finds every vulnerable pattern and fixes with flushSync where semantically required.
- [React18 Batching Fixer](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/react18-batching-fixer.agent.md): 自动批处理回归专家。React 18 会批处理所有 setState 调用，包括 Promises、setTimeout 和原生事件处理程序中的调用——React 16/17 不会。假设会立即进行中间重新渲染的带有异步状态链的类组件将产生错误状态。此代理查找每个易受攻击的模式，并在语义需要时使用 flushSync 进行修复。
- [React18 Class Surgeon](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/react18-class-surgeon.agent.md): Class component migration specialist for React 16/17 → 18.3.1. Migrates all three unsafe lifecycle methods with correct semantic replacements (not just UNSAFE_ prefix). Migrates legacy context to createContext, string refs to React.createRef(), findDOMNode to direct refs, and ReactDOM.render to createRoot. Uses memory to checkpoint per-file progress.
- [React18 Class Surgeon](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/agents/react18-class-surgeon.agent.md): React 16/17 → 18.3.1 的类组件迁移专家。使用正确的语义替换（不仅仅是 UNSAFE_ 前缀）迁移所有三个不安全的生命周期方法。将遗留上下文迁移到 createContext、字符串引用迁移到 React.createRef()、findDOMNode 迁移到直接引用、ReactDOM.render 迁移到 createRoot。使用内存来记录每个文件的进度检查点。

Rewrites every deprecated React pattern to React 19 APIs - forwardRef, defaultProps, ReactDOM.render, legacy context, string refs, useRef(). Uses memory to checkpoint progress per file. Never touches test files. Returns zero-deprecated-pattern confirmation to commander.

Does not stop until npm test reports 0 failures. Invoked as a subagent by react19-commander.

- [Self Explanatory Code Commenting](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/self-explanatory-code-commenting.instructions.md): Guidelines for GitHub Copilot to write comments to achieve self-explanatory code with less comments. - [Update Code From Shorthand](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/update-code-from-shorthand.instructions.md): Shorthand code will be in the file provided from the prompt or raw data in the prompt, and will be used to update the code file when the prompt has the text `UPDATE CODE FROM SHORTHAND`.
- [从简写更新代码](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/update-code-from-shorthand.instructions.md)：简写代码将出现在提示提供的文件或提示中的原始数据中，当提示包含文本 `UPDATE CODE FROM SHORTHAND` 时，用于更新代码文件。
- [Update Docs On Code Change](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/update-docs-on-code-change.instructions.md): Automatically update README.md and documentation files when application code changes require documentation updates
- [代码变更时更新文档](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/update-docs-on-code-change.instructions.md)：当应用代码变更需要文档更新时，自动更新 README.md 和文档文件
- [Use Cliche Data In Docs](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/use-cliche-data-in-docs.instructions.md): Ensure documentation and examples use only generic, cliche placeholder data — never real or sensitive data sourced from local scripts, configuration, task files, or prompt context.
- [在文档中使用通用数据](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/use-cliche-data-in-docs.instructions.md)：确保文档和示例仅使用通用的、常见的占位符数据 — 永远不使用来自本地脚本、配置、任务文件或提示上下文的真实或敏感数据。
- [Vsixtoolkit](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/vsixtoolkit.instructions.md): Guidelines for Visual Studio extension (VSIX) development using Community.VisualStudio.Toolkit
- [VSIX 工具包](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/vsixtoolkit.instructions.md)：使用 Community.VisualStudio.Toolkit 进行 Visual Studio 扩展（VSIX）开发的指南
- [Winui3](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/instructions/winui3.instructions.md): WinUI 3 and Windows App SDK coding guidelines. Prevents common UWP API misuse, enforces correct XAML namespaces, threading, windowing, and MVVM patterns for desktop Windows apps.

## Skills
## 技能

- [Acquire Codebase Knowledge](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acquire-codebase-knowledge/SKILL.md): Use this skill when the user explicitly asks to map, document, or onboard into an existing codebase. Trigger for prompts like "map this codebase", "document this architecture", "onboard me to this repo", or "create codebase docs". Do not trigger for routine feature implementation, bug fixes, or narrow code edits unless the user asks for repository-level discovery.
- [获取代码库知识](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acquire-codebase-knowledge/SKILL.md)：当用户明确要求映射、记录或加入现有代码库时使用此技能。针对"映射此代码库"、"记录此架构"、"帮我上手此仓库"或"创建代码库文档"等提示触发。除非用户要求仓库级别的发现，否则不要在常规功能实现、错误修复或窄范围代码编辑时触发。
- [Acreadiness Assess](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acreadiness-assess/SKILL.md): Run the AgentRC readiness assessment on the current repository and produce a static HTML dashboard at reports/index.html. Wraps `npx github:microsoft/agentrc readiness` and hands off rendering to the @ai-readiness-reporter custom agent. Supports policies (--policy) for org-specific scoring. Use when asked to assess, audit, or score the AI readiness of a repo.
- [AI 就绪性评估](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acreadiness-assess/SKILL.md)：在当前仓库上运行 AgentRC 就绪性评估，并在 reports/index.html 生成静态 HTML 仪表板。封装 `npx github:microsoft/agentrc readiness` 并将渲染移交给 @ai-readiness-reporter 自定义代理。支持策略（--policy）用于组织特定的评分。当被要求评估、审计或对仓库的 AI 就绪性进行评分时使用。
- [Acreadiness Generate Instructions](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acreadiness-generate-instructions/SKILL.md): Generate tailored AI agent instruction files via AgentRC instructions command. Produces .github/copilot-instructions.md (default, recommended for Copilot in VS Code) plus optional per-area .instructions.md files with applyTo globs for monorepos. Use after running /acreadiness-assess to close gaps in the AI Tooling pillar.
- [AI 就绪性生成指令](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acreadiness-generate-instructions/SKILL.md)：通过 AgentRC 指令命令生成定制的 AI 代理指令文件。生成 .github/copilot-instructions.md（默认，推荐用于 VS Code 中的 Copilot）以及可选的按区域 .instructions.md 文件（带有 applyTo glob 模式，适用于 monorepo）。在运行 /acreadiness-assess 后使用，以弥补 AI 工具支柱中的差距。
- [Acreadiness Policy](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acreadiness-policy/SKILL.md): Help the user pick, write, or apply an AgentRC policy. Policies customise readiness scoring by disabling irrelevant checks, overriding impact/level, setting pass-rate thresholds, or chaining org baselines with team overrides. Use when the user asks about strict mode, AI-only scoring, custom weights, CI gating, or wants org-wide standardisation.
- [AI 就绪性策略](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/acreadiness-policy/SKILL.md)：帮助用户选择、编写或应用 AgentRC 策略。策略通过禁用不相关的检查、覆盖影响/级别、设置通过率阈值或将组织基线与团队覆盖链接来自定义就绪性评分。当用户询问严格模式、仅 AI 评分、自定义权重、CI 门控或需要组织范围的标准化时使用。
- [Add Educational Comments](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/add-educational-comments/SKILL.md): Add educational comments to the file specified, or prompt asking for file to comment if one is not provided.
- [添加教育性注释](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/add-educational-comments/SKILL.md)：为指定文件添加教育性注释，如果未提供文件则提示用户选择文件。
- [Adobe Illustrator Scripting](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/adobe-illustrator-scripting/SKILL.md): Write, debug, and optimize Adobe Illustrator automation scripts using ExtendScript (JavaScript/JSX). Use when creating or modifying scripts that manipulate documents, layers, paths, text frames, colors, symbols, artboards, or any Illustrator DOM objects. Covers the complete JavaScript object model, coordinate system, measurement units, export workflows, and scripting best practices.
- [Adobe Illustrator 脚本编写](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/adobe-illustrator-scripting/SKILL.md)：使用 ExtendScript（JavaScript/JSX）编写、调试和优化 Adobe Illustrator 自动化脚本。当创建或修改操作文档、图层、路径、文本框、颜色、符号、画板或任何 Illustrator DOM 对象的脚本时使用。涵盖完整的 JavaScript 对象模型、坐标系、测量单位、导出工作流和脚本编写最佳实践。
- [Agent Governance](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agent-governance/SKILL.md): Patterns and techniques for adding governance, safety, and trust controls to AI agent systems. Use this skill when: - Building AI agents that call external tools (APIs, databases, file systems) - Implementing policy-based access controls for agent tool usage - Adding semantic intent classification to detect dangerous prompts - Creating trust scoring systems for multi-agent workflows - Building audit trails for agent actions and decisions - Enforcing rate limits, content filters, or tool restrictions on agents - Working with any agent framework (PydanticAI, CrewAI, OpenAI Agents, LangChain, AutoGen)
- [代理治理](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agent-governance/SKILL.md)：为 AI 代理系统添加治理、安全和信任控制的模式和技术。在以下情况下使用此技能：- 构建调用外部工具（API、数据库、文件系统）的 AI 代理 - 为代理工具使用实现基于策略的访问控制 - 添加语义意图分类以检测危险提示 - 为多代理工作流创建信任评分系统 - 为代理操作和决策构建审计跟踪 - 对代理执行速率限制、内容过滤器或工具限制 - 使用任何代理框架（PydanticAI、CrewAI、OpenAI Agents、LangChain、AutoGen）
- [Agent Owasp Compliance](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agent-owasp-compliance/SKILL.md): Check any AI agent codebase against the OWASP Agentic Security Initiative (ASI) Top 10 risks. Use this skill when: - Evaluating an agent system's security posture before production deployment - Running a compliance check against OWASP ASI 2026 standards - Mapping existing security controls to the 10 agentic risks - Generating a compliance report for security review or audit - Comparing agent framework security features against the standard - Any request like "is my agent OWASP compliant?", "check ASI compliance", or "agentic security audit"
- [代理 OWASP 合规性](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agent-owasp-compliance/SKILL.md)：根据 OWASP 代理安全倡议（ASI）Top 10 风险检查任何 AI 代理代码库。在以下情况下使用此技能：- 在生产部署前评估代理系统的安全态势 - 根据 OWASP ASI 2026 标准运行合规性检查 - 将现有安全控制映射到 10 个代理风险 - 为安全审查或审计生成合规性报告 - 将代理框架安全功能与标准进行比较 - 任何类似"我的代理是否符合 OWASP？"、"检查 ASI 合规性"或"代理安全审计"的请求
- [Agent Supply Chain](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agent-supply-chain/SKILL.md): Verify supply chain integrity for AI agent plugins, tools, and dependencies. Use this skill when: - Generating SHA-256 integrity manifests for agent plugins or tool packages - Verifying that installed plugins match their published manifests - Detecting tampered, modified, or untracked files in agent tool directories - Auditing dependency pinning and version policies for agent components - Building provenance chains for agent plugin promotion (dev → staging → production) - Any request like "verify plugin integrity", "generate manifest", "check supply chain", or "sign this plugin"
- [代理供应链](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agent-supply-chain/SKILL.md)：验证 AI 代理插件、工具和依赖项的供应链完整性。在以下情况下使用此技能：- 为代理插件或工具包生成 SHA-256 完整性清单 - 验证已安装的插件是否与其发布的清单匹配 - 检测代理工具目录中被篡改、修改或未跟踪的文件 - 审计代理组件的依赖固定和版本策略 - 为代理插件晋升（开发 → 预发布 → 生产）构建来源链 - 任何类似"验证插件完整性"、"生成清单"、"检查供应链"或"签名此插件"的请求
- [Agentic Eval](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agentic-eval/SKILL.md): Patterns and techniques for evaluating and improving AI agent outputs. Use this skill when: - Implementing self-critique and reflection loops - Building evaluator-optimizer pipelines for quality-critical generation - Creating test-driven code refinement workflows - Designing rubric-based or LLM-as-judge evaluation systems - Adding iterative improvement to agent outputs (code, reports, analysis) - Measuring and improving agent response quality
- [代理评估](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/agentic-eval/SKILL.md)：评估和改进 AI 代理输出的模式和技术。在以下情况下使用此技能：- 实现自我批评和反思循环 - 为质量关键的生成构建评估器-优化器管道 - 创建测试驱动的代码改进工作流 - 设计基于评分标准或 LLM 即评审的评估系统 - 为代理输出（代码、报告、分析）添加迭代改进 - 衡量和改进代理响应质量
- [Ai Prompt Engineering Safety Review](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/ai-prompt-engineering-safety-review/SKILL.md): Comprehensive AI prompt engineering safety review and improvement prompt. Analyzes prompts for safety, bias, security vulnerabilities, and effectiveness while providing detailed improvement recommendations with extensive frameworks, testing methodologies, and educational content.
- [AI 提示工程安全审查](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/ai-prompt-engineering-safety-review/SKILL.md)：全面的 AI 提示工程安全审查和改进提示。分析提示的安全性、偏见、安全漏洞和有效性，同时提供详细的改进建议，包含广泛的框架、测试方法和教育内容。
- [Ai Ready](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/ai-ready/SKILL.md): Make any repo AI-ready — analyzes your codebase and generates AGENTS.md, copilot-instructions.md, CI workflows, issue templates, and more. Mines your PR review patterns and creates files customized to your stack. USE THIS SKILL when the user asks to "make this repo ai-ready", "set up AI config", or "prepare this repo for AI contributions".

Contains every grep pattern needed to find deprecated APIs, removed APIs, unsafe lifecycle methods, batching vulnerabilities, test file issues, dependency conflicts, and React 19 specific removals. Always use this skill when writing audit scan commands - do not rely on memory for grep syntax, especially for the multi-line async setState patterns which require context flags.
- [React 审计 Grep 模式](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react-audit-grep-patterns/SKILL.md)：提供完整且经过验证的 grep 扫描命令库，用于在 React 18.3.1 或 React 19 升级之前审计 React 代码库。在运行迁移审计时使用此技能——适用于 react18-auditor 和 react19-auditor 代理。包含查找已弃用 API、已移除 API、不安全的生命周期方法、批处理漏洞、测试文件问题、依赖冲突以及 React 19 特定移除项所需的所有 grep 模式。编写审计扫描命令时务必使用此技能——不要依赖记忆来写 grep 语法，尤其是需要上下文标志的多行异步 setState 模式。
- [React18 Batching Patterns](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-batching-patterns/SKILL.md): Provides exact patterns for diagnosing and fixing automatic batching regressions in React 18 class components. Use this skill whenever a class component has multiple setState calls in an async method, inside setTimeout, inside a Promise .then() or .catch(), or in a native event handler. Use it before writing any flushSync call - the decision tree here prevents unnecessary flushSync overuse. Also use this skill when fixing test failures caused by intermediate state assertions that break after React 18 upgrade.
- [React18 批处理模式](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-batching-patterns/SKILL.md)：提供用于诊断和修复 React 18 类组件中自动批处理回归问题的精确模式。当类组件在异步方法、setTimeout、Promise .then() 或 .catch() 或原生事件处理程序中有多个 setState 调用时使用此技能。在编写任何 flushSync 调用之前使用它——此处的决策树可防止 flushSync 的不必要过度使用。在修复因 React 18 升级后中间状态断言失败导致的测试失败时也可使用此技能。

- [React18 Enzyme To Rtl](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-enzyme-to-rtl/SKILL.md): Provides exact Enzyme → React Testing Library migration patterns for React 18 upgrades. Use this skill whenever Enzyme tests need to be rewritten - shallow, mount, wrapper.find(), wrapper.simulate(), wrapper.prop(), wrapper.state(), wrapper.instance(), Enzyme configure/Adapter calls, or any test file that imports from enzyme. This skill covers the full API mapping and the philosophy shift from implementation testing to behavior testing. Always read this skill before rewriting Enzyme tests - do not translate Enzyme APIs 1:1, that produces brittle RTL tests.
- [React18 Enzyme 转 RTL](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-enzyme-to-rtl/SKILL.md)：为 React 18 升级提供精确的 Enzyme → React Testing Library 迁移模式。当需要重写 Enzyme 测试时使用此技能——包括 shallow、mount、wrapper.find()、wrapper.simulate()、wrapper.prop()、wrapper.state()、wrapper.instance()、Enzyme configure/Adapter 调用，或任何从 enzyme 导入的测试文件。此技能涵盖完整的 API 映射以及从实现测试到行为测试的理念转变。在重写 Enzyme 测试之前务必阅读此技能——不要将 Enzyme API 1:1 直译，那样会产生脆弱的 RTL 测试。
- [React18 Legacy Context](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-legacy-context/SKILL.md): Provides the complete migration pattern for React legacy context API (contextTypes, childContextTypes, getChildContext) to the modern createContext API. Use this skill whenever migrating legacy context in class components - this is always a cross-file migration requiring the provider AND all consumers to be updated together. Use it before touching any contextTypes or childContextTypes code, because migrating only the provider without the consumers (or vice versa) will cause a runtime failure. Always read this skill before writing any context migration - the cross-file coordination steps here prevent the most common context migration bugs.
- [React18 旧版 Context](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-legacy-context/SKILL.md)：提供 React 旧版 context API（contextTypes、childContextTypes、getChildContext）到现代 createContext API 的完整迁移模式。在类组件中迁移旧版 context 时使用此技能——这始终是一个跨文件迁移，需要同时更新提供者和所有消费者。在接触任何 contextTypes 或 childContextTypes 代码之前使用它，因为仅迁移提供者而不迁移消费者（反之亦然）将导致运行时失败。在编写任何 context 迁移之前务必阅读此技能——此处的跨文件协调步骤可防止最常见的 context 迁移缺陷。

Use this skill whenever a class component needs its lifecycle methods migrated, when deciding between getDerivedStateFromProps vs componentDidUpdate, when adding getSnapshotBeforeUpdate, or when fixing React 18 UNSAFE_ lifecycle warnings. - [React18 生命周期模式](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/react18-lifecycle-patterns/SKILL.md)：提供三个不安全的类组件生命周期方法——componentWillMount、componentWillReceiveProps 和 componentWillUpdate——的精确迁移前后模式，目标为 React 18.3.1。当类组件需要迁移其生命周期方法、在 getDerivedStateFromProps 与 componentDidUpdate 之间做决定、添加 getSnapshotBeforeUpdate 或修复 React 18 UNSAFE_ 生命周期警告时使用此技能。在编写任何生命周期迁移代码之前务必使用此技能——不要凭记忆猜测模式，此处的决策树可防止最常见的迁移错误。

Use this skill whenever migrating string ref usage - including single element refs, multiple refs in a component, refs in lists, callback refs, and refs passed to child components. - [Terraform AzureRM Set 差异分析器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/terraform-azurerm-set-diff-analyzer/SKILL.md)：分析 AzureRM 提供程序的 Terraform plan JSON 输出，以区分误报差异（Set 类型属性中的仅顺序变更）和实际资源变更。在审查 Azure 资源（如应用程序网关、负载均衡器、防火墙、Front Door、NSG 及其他具有 Set 类型属性的、因内部排序变更导致虚假差异的资源）的 terraform plan 输出时使用。
- [Threat Model Analyst](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/threat-model-analyst/SKILL.md): Full STRIDE-A threat model analysis and incremental update skill for repositories and systems. Supports two modes: (1) Single analysis — full STRIDE-A threat model of a repository, producing architecture overviews, DFD diagrams, STRIDE-A analysis, prioritized findings, and executive assessments. (2) Incremental analysis — takes a previous threat model report as baseline, compares the codebase at the latest (or a given commit), and produces an updated report with change tracking (new, resolved, still-present threats), STRIDE heatmap, findings diff, and an embedded HTML comparison. Only activate when the user explicitly requests a threat model analysis, incremental update, or invokes /threat-model-analyst directly.
- [威胁模型分析器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/threat-model-analyst/SKILL.md)：针对仓库和系统的完整 STRIDE-A 威胁模型分析和增量更新技能。支持两种模式：(1) 单次分析——对仓库进行完整的 STRIDE-A 威胁建模，生成架构概览、DFD 图、STRIDE-A 分析、优先级发现和执行评估。(2) 增量分析——以之前的威胁模型报告为基线，比较最新（或给定提交）的代码库，并生成带有变更追踪（新增、已解决、仍存在的威胁）、STRIDE 热力图、发现差异和嵌入式 HTML 对比的更新报告。仅在用户明确请求威胁模型分析、增量更新或直接调用 /threat-model-analyst 时激活。
- [Tldr Prompt](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/tldr-prompt/SKILL.md): Create tldr summaries for GitHub Copilot files (prompts, agents, instructions, collections), MCP servers, or documentation from URLs and queries.
- [TLDR 提示](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/tldr-prompt/SKILL.md)：为 GitHub Copilot 文件（提示、代理、指令、集合）、MCP 服务器或文档从 URL 和查询创建太长不看版摘要。
- [Transloadit Media Processing](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/transloadit-media-processing/SKILL.md): Process media files (video, audio, images, documents) using Transloadit. Use when asked to encode video to HLS/MP4, generate thumbnails, resize or watermark images, extract audio, concatenate clips, add subtitles, OCR documents, or run any media processing pipeline. Covers 86+ processing robots for file transformation at scale.
- [Transloadit 媒体处理](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/transloadit-media-processing/SKILL.md)：使用 Transloadit 处理媒体文件（视频、音频、图像、文档）。当被要求将视频编码为 HLS/MP4、生成缩略图、调整图像大小或添加水印、提取音频、拼接片段、添加字幕、OCR 文档或运行任何媒体处理管线时使用。涵盖 86+ 个用于大规模文件转换的处理机器人。
- [Typescript Mcp Server Generator](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typescript-mcp-server-generator/SKILL.md): Generate a complete MCP server project in TypeScript with tools, resources, and proper configuration
- [TypeScript MCP 服务器生成器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typescript-mcp-server-generator/SKILL.md)：生成完整的 TypeScript MCP 服务器项目，包含工具、资源和正确的配置
- [Typespec Api Operations](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typespec-api-operations/SKILL.md): Add GET, POST, PATCH, and DELETE operations to a TypeSpec API plugin with proper routing, parameters, and adaptive cards
- [TypeSpec API 操作](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typespec-api-operations/SKILL.md)：为 TypeSpec API 插件添加 GET、POST、PATCH 和 DELETE 操作，包含正确的路由、参数和自适应卡片
- [Typespec Create Agent](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typespec-create-agent/SKILL.md): Generate a complete TypeSpec declarative agent with instructions, capabilities, and conversation starters for Microsoft 365 Copilot
- [TypeSpec 创建代理](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typespec-create-agent/SKILL.md)：为 Microsoft 365 Copilot 生成完整的 TypeSpec 声明式代理，包含指令、功能和对话启动器
- [Typespec Create Api Plugin](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typespec-create-api-plugin/SKILL.md): Generate a TypeSpec API plugin with REST operations, authentication, and Adaptive Cards for Microsoft 365 Copilot
- [TypeSpec 创建 API 插件](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/typespec-create-api-plugin/SKILL.md)：为 Microsoft 365 Copilot 生成具有 REST 操作、身份验证和自适应卡片的 TypeSpec API 插件
- [Unit Test Vue Pinia](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/unit-test-vue-pinia/SKILL.md): Write and review unit tests for Vue 3 + TypeScript + Vitest + Pinia codebases. Use when creating or updating tests for components, composables, and stores; mocking Pinia with createTestingPinia; applying Vue Test Utils patterns; and enforcing black-box assertions over implementation details.
- [Vue Pinia 单元测试](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/unit-test-vue-pinia/SKILL.md)：为 Vue 3 + TypeScript + Vitest + Pinia 代码库编写和审查单元测试。在创建或更新组件、可组合函数和 store 的测试、使用 createTestingPinia 模拟 Pinia、应用 Vue Test Utils 模式以及强制对实现细节使用黑盒断言时使用。
- [Update Avm Modules In Bicep](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-avm-modules-in-bicep/SKILL.md): Update Azure Verified Modules (AVM) to latest versions in Bicep files.
- [更新 Bicep 中的 AVM 模块](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-avm-modules-in-bicep/SKILL.md)：将 Bicep 文件中的 Azure 验证模块 (AVM) 更新到最新版本。
- [Update Implementation Plan](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-implementation-plan/SKILL.md): Update an existing implementation plan file with new or update requirements to provide new features, refactoring existing code or upgrading packages, design, architecture or infrastructure.
- [更新实现计划](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-implementation-plan/SKILL.md)：使用新的或更新的需求更新现有实现计划文件，以提供新功能、重构现有代码或升级包、设计、架构或基础设施。
- [Update Llms](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-llms/SKILL.md): Update the llms.txt file in the root folder to reflect changes in documentation or specifications following the llms.txt specification at https://llmstxt.org/
- [更新 llms](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-llms/SKILL.md)：更新根文件夹中的 llms.txt 文件以反映文档或规范的变更，遵循 https://llmstxt.org/ 上的 llms.txt 规范

- [Update Specification](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-specification/SKILL.md): Update an existing specification file for the solution, optimized for Generative AI consumption based on new requirements or updates to any existing code.
- [更新规范](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/update-specification/SKILL.md)：更新解决方案的现有规范文件，基于新需求或对任何现有代码的更新进行优化，以便生成式 AI 消费。
- [Vardoger Analyze](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/vardoger-analyze/SKILL.md): Use when the user asks to personalize the GitHub Copilot CLI assistant, adapt Copilot to their style, use vardoger, or analyze their Copilot CLI conversation history. Reads the local session directory at `~/.copilot/session-state/`, extracts recurring preferences and conventions, and writes a fenced personalization block into `~/.copilot/copilot-instructions.md`. Runs entirely on the user's machine via the local `vardoger` CLI (`pipx install vardoger`); no network calls and no uploads. Triggers: 'personalize my copilot', 'analyze my copilot history', 'tailor copilot to me', 'run vardoger', 'update my copilot instructions from history', 'make copilot learn my style'.
- [Vardoger 分析](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/vardoger-analyze/SKILL.md)：当用户要求个性化 GitHub Copilot CLI 助手、让 Copilot 适应其风格、使用 vardoger 或分析其 Copilot CLI 对话历史时使用。读取 `~/.copilot/session-state/` 中的本地会话目录，提取重复出现的偏好和约定，并将一个隔离的个性化块写入 `~/.copilot/copilot-instructions.md`。完全通过本地 `vardoger` CLI（`pipx install vardoger`）在用户机器上运行；无网络调用和上传。触发条件："个性化我的 copilot"、"分析我的 copilot 历史"、"为我定制 copilot"、"运行 vardoger"、"从历史更新我的 copilot 指令"、"让 copilot 学习我的风格"。
- [Vscode Ext Commands](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/vscode-ext-commands/SKILL.md): Guidelines for contributing commands in VS Code extensions. Indicates naming convention, visibility, localization and other relevant attributes, following VS Code extension development guidelines, libraries and good practices
- [VS Code 扩展命令](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/vscode-ext-commands/SKILL.md)：VS Code 扩展中贡献命令的指南。说明命名约定、可见性、本地化和其他相关属性，遵循 VS Code 扩展开发指南、库和最佳实践
- [Vscode Ext Localization](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/vscode-ext-localization/SKILL.md): Guidelines for proper localization of VS Code extensions, following VS Code extension development guidelines, libraries and good practices
- [VS Code 扩展本地化](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/vscode-ext-localization/SKILL.md)：VS Code 扩展正确本地化的指南，遵循 VS Code 扩展开发指南、库和最佳实践
- [Web Coder](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/web-coder/SKILL.md): Expert 10x engineer with comprehensive knowledge of web development, internet protocols, and web standards. Use when working with HTML, CSS, JavaScript, web APIs, HTTP/HTTPS, web security, performance optimization, accessibility, or any web/internet concepts. Specializes in translating web terminology accurately and implementing modern web standards across frontend and backend development.
- [Web 编码器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/web-coder/SKILL.md)：具备 Web 开发、互联网协议和 Web 标准全面知识的专家级 10x 工程师。在处理 HTML、CSS、JavaScript、Web API、HTTP/HTTPS、Web 安全、性能优化、无障碍性或任何 Web/互联网概念时使用。专精于准确翻译 Web 术语并在前端和后端开发中实现现代 Web 标准。
- [Web Design Reviewer](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/web-design-reviewer/SKILL.md): This skill enables visual inspection of websites running locally or remotely to identify and fix design issues. Triggers on requests like "review website design", "check the UI", "fix the layout", "find design problems". Detects issues with responsive design, accessibility, visual consistency, and layout breakage, then performs fixes at the source code level.
- [Web 设计审查器](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/web-design-reviewer/SKILL.md)：此技能可对本地或远程运行的网站进行视觉检查，以识别和修复设计问题。在"审查网站设计"、"检查 UI"、"修复布局"、"查找设计问题"等请求时触发。检测响应式设计、无障碍性、视觉一致性和布局破坏问题，然后在源代码层面执行修复。
- [Webapp Testing](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/webapp-testing/SKILL.md): Toolkit for interacting with and testing local web applications using Playwright. Supports verifying frontend functionality, debugging UI behavior, capturing browser screenshots, and viewing browser logs.
- [Web 应用测试](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/webapp-testing/SKILL.md)：使用 Playwright 与本地 Web 应用交互和测试的工具包。支持验证前端功能、调试 UI 行为、捕获浏览器截图和查看浏览器日志。
- [What Context Needed](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/what-context-needed/SKILL.md): Ask Copilot what files it needs to see before answering a question
- [需要什么上下文](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/what-context-needed/SKILL.md)：在回答问题之前询问 Copilot 需要查看哪些文件
- [Winapp Cli](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/winapp-cli/SKILL.md): Windows App Development CLI (winapp) for building, packaging, signing, debugging, and UI-automating Windows applications. Use when asked to initialize Windows app projects, create MSIX packages, manage AppxManifest.xml or development certificates, run an app as packaged for debugging, automate Windows UI via Microsoft UI Automation, publish to the Microsoft Store, or access Windows SDK build tools. Covers commands like init, pack, run, unregister, manifest, cert, sign, store, ui, and tool. Supports .NET (csproj), C++, Electron, Rust, Tauri, Flutter, and other Windows frameworks.
- [Winapp CLI](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/winapp-cli/SKILL.md)：用于构建、打包、签名、调试和 UI 自动化 Windows 应用程序的 Windows 应用开发 CLI (winapp)。当被要求初始化 Windows 应用项目、创建 MSIX 包、管理 AppxManifest.xml 或开发证书、以打包形式运行应用进行调试、通过 Microsoft UI Automation 自动化 Windows UI、发布到 Microsoft Store 或访问 Windows SDK 构建工具时使用。涵盖 init、pack、run、unregister、manifest、cert、sign、store、ui 和 tool 等命令。支持 .NET (csproj)、C++、Electron、Rust、Tauri、Flutter 和其他 Windows 框架。
- [Winmd Api Search](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/winmd-api-search/SKILL.md): Find and explore Windows desktop APIs. Use when building features that need platform capabilities — camera, file access, notifications, UI controls, AI/ML, sensors, networking, etc. Discovers the right API for a task and retrieves full type details (methods, properties, events, enumeration values).
- [Winmd API 搜索](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/winmd-api-search/SKILL.md)：查找和探索 Windows 桌面 API。在构建需要平台能力的功能时使用——摄像头、文件访问、通知、UI 控件、AI/ML、传感器、网络等。发现适合任务的 API 并检索完整的类型详情（方法、属性、事件、枚举值）。
- [Winui3 Migration Guide](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/winui3-migration-guide/SKILL.md): UWP-to-WinUI 3 migration reference. Maps legacy UWP APIs to correct Windows App SDK equivalents with before/after code snippets. Covers namespace changes, threading (CoreDispatcher to DispatcherQueue), windowing (CoreWindow to AppWindow), dialogs, pickers, sharing, printing, background tasks, and the most common Copilot code generation mistakes.
- [WinUI 3 迁移指南](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/winui3-migration-guide/SKILL.md)：UWP 到 WinUI 3 的迁移参考。将旧版 UWP API 映射到正确的 Windows App SDK 等效项，并提供前后代码片段。涵盖命名空间变更、线程（CoreDispatcher 到 DispatcherQueue）、窗口（CoreWindow 到 AppWindow）、对话框、选择器、共享、打印、后台任务以及最常见的 Copilot 代码生成错误。
- [Workiq Copilot](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/workiq-copilot/SKILL.md): Guides the Copilot CLI on how to use the WorkIQ CLI/MCP server to query Microsoft 365 Copilot data (emails, meetings, docs, Teams, people) for live context, summaries, and recommendations.
- [WorkIQ Copilot](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/workiq-copilot/SKILL.md)：指导 Copilot CLI 如何使用 WorkIQ CLI/MCP 服务器查询 Microsoft 365 Copilot 数据（邮件、会议、文档、Teams、人员）以获取实时上下文、摘要和建议。
- [Write Coding Standards From File](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/write-coding-standards-from-file/SKILL.md): Write a coding standards document for a project using the coding styles from the file(s) and/or folder(s) passed as arguments in the prompt.
- [从文件编写编码标准](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/write-coding-standards-from-file/SKILL.md)：使用提示中作为参数传递的文件和/或文件夹中的编码风格为项目编写编码标准文档。
- [X Twitter Scraper](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/x-twitter-scraper/SKILL.md): Build GitHub Copilot workflows with Xquik X API SDKs, REST endpoints, MCP tools, signed webhooks, tweet search, user lookup, follower exports, media actions, and agent automation.
- [X Twitter 爬虫](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/github/awesome-copilot/main/skills/x-twitter-scraper/SKILL.md)：使用 Xquik X API SDK、REST 端点、MCP 工具、签名 Webhook、推文搜索、用户查找、粉丝导出、媒体操作和代理自动化构建 GitHub Copilot 工作流。
